It’s also possible to have GPS position continues.\r\nThere is also a search function to find places and locations on the map or from your loaded pois.\r\nIt is fully customizable for startup and home position and zoom levels. \r\nYou can use POI Viewer offline with maps and local copy of your files (after download of maps).\r\nPoiViewer10 can read GPS exchange format .gpx (Waypoints, Routes and Tracks), Garmin, .fit and .tcx files, Google Maps .kml and .kmz (Placemarks, Lines and Polygons), text files .csv and Tomtom .ov2 files.\r\nSupport png and bmp Icon file to poi file, and support for embedded Icons for kml and kmz files.\r\nIt's possible to open driving- and walking instructions and a point on the Windows mapping program. \r\nYou can record of your movements in a track on the map.
